# Design Coverage Manifest

Every concrete deliverable from `DESIGN.md`, mapped to the phase it lands in and its current status.

**Status legend**:
- тЬЕ **DONE** тАФ fully implemented and verified
- ЁЯЯб **PARTIAL** тАФ data/scaffolding exists, behavior pending later phase
- тП│ **PENDING** тАФ not started, scheduled
- ЁЯТн **OPEN** тАФ open-ended ("many more X" тАФ track count over time)

**Phase exit ritual** (what I MUST do before declaring a phase complete):
1. Read this file end-to-end.
2. For every row tagged with the current phase, verify status against the codebase.
3. If anything tagged for this phase is still PENDING or PARTIAL, fix it or explicitly defer with the user's approval before marking the phase complete.
4. Update statuses in this file whenever a row's state changes.

**Last full audit**: 2026-05-27 (**Spectra fleshed out from teaser to full companion + new `flawless_reign` achievement.** Sixth fully-built companion landed: ghost-girl otaku with 113 sprites baked under 66 semantic expression IDs, runtime variant rotation, 25% ghost-flicker opacity overlay, 627-line dialogue bank covering all categories + 100% specifics. Unlocked via the new `flawless_reign` legendary (30 days no-hit, title "The Flawless"). Two reusable systems added that any future companion can opt into: `variantGroups` (semantic-id тЖТ variant-file rotation in NpcCompanion + ArchetypeDecorOverlay) and `ghostFlickerRate` / `solidOnlyExpressions` (per-companion translucency overlay). `BossSystem._applyDamageToBoss` now emits `BOSS_DAMAGED` so the no-hit metric tracker covers every HP-loss path. Prior audit:** 2026-05-26 (**Achievements popup conversion + leaderboard view overhaul + legendary toast pass.** Big visual + structural pass driven by user iteration through this session. Twelve new Section 41 rows landed, all тЬЕ DONE: **`ach-popup-conversion`** тАФ AchievementsOverlay converted from a full-screen panel to a centered popup using the shared `Overlay` shell (1300├Ч840, gold accent, unfurl animation), matching `LeaderboardOverlay`'s dimensions so the two read as sibling Hall-of-X popups. `_render` тЖТ `_renderBody` returns just inner content; the shell provides backdrop + close X + Esc + backdrop-click. Header z-index bumped to 20 so the title-picker dropdown paints above tabs/recent/view-wrap. Title centered in the shell's header bar via `:has(.qf-ach)` selector тАФ scoped so other overlays keep their left-aligned titles. Grid forced to 3 columns with `repeat(3, minmax(0, 1fr))` (the canonical fix for unequal CSS grid columns when one card has a wider non-wrapping chip). View-wrap padding bumped to 24px each side to clear the shell's ~18px inset gold frame. **`ach-reward-aware-icons`** тАФ icon medal color driven by `data-reward-type` (boss/companion/title/recognition) instead of category. Pure-recognition cards get cream icons; reward-bearing cards adopt their reward chip's color. Creates a per-card two-tone read тАФ colored border (category) ├Ч colored medal (reward type). With the move to emoji icons (next row), the icon glyph itself uses OS-native emoji colors, but the icon badge BORDER still inherits the reward-type color so the signal isn't lost. **`ach-lb-podium-rich`** тАФ achievement leaderboard's podium upgraded from simple [badge + name + count] to the FULL triptych matching the main run-leaderboard: [companion sprite \| floating #N badge + boss portrait + player name + title chip + trophy count \| stats block]. DOM order `[#2, #1, #3]` with `1fr 1.2fr 1fr` columns + `align-items: end` so cards step UPWARD in a proper podium silhouette (200/170/140px heights). Companion sprite + boss portrait + active-title chip all gracefully degrade for rows that predate those fields. `_loadLeaderboard` extended to extract companionId/bossLevel/days/kills/activeTitle. **`ach-lb-achievement-stats`** тАФ podium stats block content rewritten from RUN stats (BOSS LV / DAYS / KILLS тАФ wrong context) to achievement-derived TITLES / BOSSES / COMPANIONS counts decoded from `achievementBits`, color-coded by reward type. Totals reflect "total ACCESS" (starters + achievement-unlocked) тАФ BOSSES = 3 starters + X / 12 total, COMPANIONS = 3 starters + X / 4 total. **`ach-lb-trophy-block`** тАФ headline trophy count upgraded from plain text to a styled block with rank-colored big number (28/22/20px per rank), soft glow, smaller denominator, and a 5px progress bar showing % unlocked. **`ach-lb-empty-state`** тАФ YOUR-RANK band always renders even when the leaderboard is empty so the player sees their own count regardless of remote data; mango shows "EXCLUDED (CHEAT)" in the band; context-aware empty message explains why the board is empty for mango. **`ach-lb-placeholder-podium`** тАФ podium ALWAYS renders 3 slots; missing ranks show inert "AWAITING CHALLENGER" placeholders so the layout doesn't read broken on sparse boards. **`ach-lb-global-stats`** тАФ new stats panel below the ranked list (TOTAL KEEPERS / AVG TROPHIES / RAREST TROPHY / MOST POPULAR TITLE) computed from in-memory data, fills the dead zone below sparse boards + adds permanent global context. **`ach-lb-viewer-leaderboard-hide`** тАФ LEADERBOARD destination button hidden in viewer mode (drilled into another player's grid) тАФ avoids confusing nesting + frees the slot for the COMPARE WITH YOU toggle. **`ach-compare-toggle-inline`** тАФ compare toggle moved from `position: absolute; top: 30px; right: 24px` (a relic of the full-screen layout that put it on top of the LEADERBOARD button) to inline flow in the header. **`ach-legendary-toast`** тАФ legendary unlocks (the 6 hand-picked `def.legendary: true` achievements) get a tier-aware toast: RARE TROPHY eyebrow, "LEGENDARY UNLOCKED" header, gold-bright frame with ember inset glow + 2.2s pulse, larger glyph + title, 10s dwell, plus a 22-particle gold burst fountaining leftward into the play area (CSS-keyframed, per-particle `--dx/--dy` trajectory vars, biased to a 120┬░ leftward arc since the toast sits on the right edge of the HUD). Legendary tier is now data-driven via `def.legendary` in `achievements.json` тАФ the JS reads the same flag for both grid card shimmer and toast tier branching. **`ach-title-picker-cleanup`** тАФ HIGH-severity bug found in audit: title-picker outside-click handler was leaking when the player closed the overlay while picker was open. Centralized teardown in `_onOverlayClose` (now the Overlay shell's onClose callback) tears down keydown + outside-click + nested viewer in one path. Also updated the visual-polish row's notes to reflect post-feedback iterations: padding-right on the card-col for rarity badge gutter; reward-chip nowrap with ellipsis; name color reverted to parchment cream so each card has ONE focal point (the icon medal) instead of three competing same-color elements; thematic emoji icons with U+FE0F variation selectors forcing emoji presentation on glyphs that default to monochrome. Previous audit 2026-05-26 (**Per-name storage refactor + achievements visual polish pass.** Driven by user feedback that LJ saw mango's "all unlocked" state тАФ all player-progress keys were globally-scoped, so mango's cheat writes leaked into every other account. Refactored every key to per-name (`<base>:<trimmed-name>`) matching the existing `maxBossLevel` pattern: `qf.companions.unlocked`, `qf.achievements.unlocked`, `qf.achievements.metrics`, `qf.player.titles`, `qf.achievements.timestamps`, `qf.player.active_title_id`. Legacy global keys wiped at module load (Option A тАФ no production data to migrate). `PlayerProfile.setName()` emits `NAME_CHANGED` so `AchievementSystem._reloadForCurrentPlayer()` re-hydrates without a page refresh. Mango cheat now writes only to mango's slot. Earlier the same day: visual polish pass on the achievements overlay (`ach-visual-polish` row) тАФ per-category color tokens, reward-chip semantic colors, subtle card-bg tints, title chip inherits source-category color, legendary-tier shimmer treatment for 6 hand-picked endgame achievements, per-achievement icon variety in `achievements.json`. Previous audit 2026-05-25 (**Section 41 тАФ title selection + recent unlocks + leaderboard title display.** Three new rows тЬЕ DONE: (1) **`ach-title-selection`** тАФ the active-title chip in the AchievementsOverlay header is now clickable; clicking drops a floating picker beneath with one row per unlocked title plus an `тЧЗ AUTO` option that clears the pin and resumes most-recently-unlocked auto-promotion. Persisted under new `qf.profile.activeTitleId` localStorage key (`null` = AUTO). `PlayerProfile.getActiveTitle()` now prefers the selected id and falls back to most-recent. Picker is absolutely positioned against `.qf-ach` so opening it doesn't push the header; outside-click closes it; selection patches the chip name in-place. (2) **`ach-recent-strip`** тАФ RECENT UNLOCKS strip between the tabs row and the grid in self-view, showing the 3 most-recent unlocks with relative-time labels ("12 minutes ago" / "Just now"). Driven by new `qf.achievements.timestamps` localStorage key (written by `PlayerProfile.unlockAchievement`; retroactive scan timestamps back-fill on first boot). Auto-hidden when the player has zero unlocks; viewer mode skips it (no timestamp feed for other players). (3) **`ach-lb-title-display`** тАФ active title shown on the main run-leaderboard in place of the legacy IMMORTAL / BUTCHER / CUNNING accolades. Plumbed via `meta.active_title` on the run payload; LeaderboardOverlay's `_normalize` reads it into `row.title`; podium + detail chips render `title \|\| accolade` so older rows without the field keep the legacy top-3 labels (back-compat). Chip CSS got `max-width: 160/220px` + ellipsis because the longest title is "Veteran Exterminator" (20 chars). Previous audit 2026-05-25 (**Section 41 polish + deferral close-out.** Five row additions, all тЬЕ DONE: (1) **`ach-titles`** тАФ title-reward system. 17 high-tier achievements (10 boss-level 11тАУ20 + 7 mastery / cumulative-grind) now grant a player title via a new `title` field on the achievement definition. `PlayerProfile.unlockTitle/getUnlockedTitles/getActiveTitle` persist them under `qf.player.titles`; active title auto-promotes to the most-recently-unlocked one. Surfaced as a gold-burst `тЬж TITLE ┬╖ <name>` chip in the AchievementsOverlay header (self-view only). Title-granting cards show a `тЬж Title: <name>` reward chip. (2) **`ach-true-approach-a`** тАФ boss-archetype unlocks now go through `PlayerProfile.isAchievementUnlocked(boss-level-achId)` instead of `maxBossLevel >=` direct reads. ArchetypeSelect's UNLOCK_GATES maps each archetype to its achievement id (e.g. golem тЖФ rising_power). Existing players see zero behaviour change because the retroactive scan unlocks the matching achievements on first boot. Cleaner architectural promise тАФ bosses unlock when their achievement unlocks. (3) **`ach-toast-batching`** тАФ `AchievementSystem._retroactiveScan` now does a two-pass scan: collect all unlockable achievements without firing, then queue them via setTimeout with 900ms initial delay + 700ms stagger so existing high-progress players don't get their toasts silently dropped by the ToastQueue MAX_TOASTS=4 cap. (4) **`ach-rarity`** тАФ client-side per-achievement rarity stats. Leaderboard fetch is now eager on overlay-open (was lazy until LB tab activated); ingested rows feed `AchievementSystem.ingestRarityFromRows` which computes how many players have each achievement. Cards get a small top-right badge: "5% rare" (gold-bright) for <10%, "earned" (muted) otherwise. Sample size kept alongside fraction for future tooltips. (5) **`ach-class-hunter-tune`** тАФ Class Hunter target 9 тЖТ 11 to match the count of regularly-spawnable classes in `adventurerClasses.json`. Description tightened. ## 1b. Monster boss redesign тАФ supersedes the 15-archetype system (target: 10 monster bosses)

> See DESIGN.md тЖТ "Monster boss redesign" for the locked spec per boss (one-or-two playstyle-defining abilities; no padding modifiers).
> Spec finalized 2026-05-02. Implementation in progress тАФ order is `1b.1` (Orc) тЖТ `1b.11` (Gnoll), ascending complexity / shared-infra dependencies.

| ID | Boss | Locked abilities (headline summary) | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| orc         | Orc Veteran      | **Loot the Fallen** тАФ each orc keeps +1 ATK per kill (per-orc, lost on death). **Warband** тАФ orcs in the same room give every other orc in that room +5% ATK and +5% DEF, stacks per ally, no cap. | 1b.1 / 1b.12 | тЬЕ DONE (2026-05-02 тАФ both abilities) | **Loot the Fallen (1b.1):** `BossArchetypeSystem` listens for `ADVENTURER_DIED`/`MINION_DIED` while archetype = orc + killer is an orc-tagged minion; bumps `lootAtkBonus` (no longer writes `stats.attack` directly тАФ Warband's recompute owns the live value). On death, `lootAtkBonus` is zeroed; the next `_tickOrc` pass auto-rebalances the cluster. `MinionRenderer` paints a small "+N" badge in orc-red at the bottom-left of the orc sprite (gated by archetype + tag + bonus>0). **Warband (1b.12):** `_tickOrc` runs every frame from `tick(delta)` for the orc archetype. Per orc, looks up its current room via `dungeonGrid.getRoomAtTile`, counts other live orc-tagged minions in the same room, derives `atkMult = 1 + allies ├Ч ORC_WARBAND_ATK_PCT_PER_ALLY` (0.05) and `defMult = 1 + allies ├Ч ORC_WARBAND_DEF_PCT_PER_ALLY` (0.05), then writes `stats.attack = round((_orcBaseAttack + lootAtkBonus) ├Ч atkMult)` and `stats.defense = round(_orcBaseDefense ├Ч defMult)`. Pristine baselines stamped on `MINION_PLACED`, `BOSS_LEVELED_UP` (rebaselined post-scale by inferring base from current value ├╖ live warband multiplier), and at scene boot for save-load via `_captureOrcBaseline` (subtracts active loot bonus before stamping). New balance constants: `ORC_WARBAND_ATK_PCT_PER_ALLY`, `ORC_WARBAND_DEF_PCT_PER_ALLY`. No SaveSystem changes тАФ all new fields (`_orcBaseAttack`, `_orcBaseDefense`, `lootAtkBonus`) are plain numbers that JSON-serialize naturally. |
| golem       | Earth Golem      | **Living Architecture** тАФ every placed room (incl. boss + corridor) тЖТ +5 boss HP / +1 DEF permanent. **Earthquake** тАФ 1├Ч/day day-phase button; pick a room, advs inside take (rooms placed ├Ч 2) damage. | 1b.2 | тЬЕ DONE (2026-05-02) | `BossArchetypeSystem` listens for `ROOM_PLACED`/`ROOM_REMOVED` while archetype is golem; tracks `gameState.boss._golem` (`roomsCounted` / `hpApplied` / `defApplied` / `earthquakeUsesLeft` / `firstUseToastShown`) so a save/load and dynamic place/remove stay balanced and don't double-count. On scene init, backfills any rooms not yet counted (handles old saves cleanly). Earthquake: new `BossArchetypeUI` panel above the action bar shows the EARTHQUAKE button only when archetype = golem and phase = day; click тЖТ arms; next click on a dungeon tile тЖТ resolves the room тЖТ emits `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_TARGET` тЖТ system applies `(rooms ├Ч 2)` damage to every adv inside (uses `gameState.dungeon.rooms.length`, no cap). Damage routes through `COMBAT_HIT` and triggers `ADVENTURER_DIED` if HP drops to 0 (so RunHistorySystem / boss XP still fire). UI consumes `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_FIRED` and plays a Game-camera shake (450 ms) + a floating `EARTHQUAKE -N` text over the room center. Daily uses reset on `NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED`. First-use toast fires on construction (UI-side gate via `firstUseToastShown` flag, immune to scene-startup ordering). New balance constants: `GOLEM_HP_PER_ROOM`, `GOLEM_DEF_PER_ROOM`, `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_DMG_PER_ROOM`, `GOLEM_EARTHQUAKE_USES_PER_DAY`. Click-on-button gate prevents the room-pick handler from resolving a phantom room when the player clicks the button itself to disarm. |
| beholder    | Beholder Tyrant  | **Petrify Gaze** тАФ BossFightScene only; freezes advs 2s every 6s with eye-beam VFX. **Anti-Magic Aura** тАФ 2 random rooms/day disable class abilities for the day (+1 per boss level); purple glow VFX | 1b.3 | тЬЕ DONE (2026-05-02) | Petrify Gaze: `BossArchetypeSystem` listens to `BOSS_FIGHT_STARTED` and starts a Phaser timer that fires every `BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_INTERVAL_MS` (6000) for the duration of the fight. Each fire stamps `adv._petrifiedUntil = now + BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_DURATION_MS` (2000) on every adv inside the boss chamber. `BossSystem._tickFightAdv` early-returns while petrified (freeze in place); `BossSystem._runOneRound`'s attackers filter excludes petrified advs (no boss damage that round). VFX: dedicated `_petrifyFxGraphics` layer draws eye-beams from boss to each target + stone-crackle rings on targets, fading over the 2 s freeze window (prior tweens killed before re-fire). Timer torn down on `BOSS_FIGHT_RESOLVED`; lingering `_petrifiedUntil` cleared so survivors aren't stuck. Anti-Magic Aura: `DAY_PHASE_BEGAN` triggers `_rollAntiMagicRooms` тАФ Fisher-Yates picks `BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_BASE_ROOMS` (2) + `(bossLevel-1) ├Ч BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_PER_BOSS_LV` (1) random non-boss rooms, stamps `room._antiMagic=true` and `gameState._antiMagicRoomIds=[тАж]`. `ClassAbilitySystem.update` reads the daily set and skips the `consider*(adv)` switch when an adv stands inside a marked room (existing buffs still tick out via `_tickActiveBuffs`). VFX: `_antiMagicFx` graphics layer paints a soft purple wash + bright outline on each marked room. `NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED` clears marks + the overlay. Save/load safe тАФ both per-room flags and the gameState id list serialize naturally; constructor calls `_renderAntiMagicAura` so a mid-day reload still shows the glow. New balance constants: `BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_INTERVAL_MS`, `BEHOLDER_PETRIFY_DURATION_MS`, `BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_BASE_ROOMS`, `BEHOLDER_ANTIMAGIC_PER_BOSS_LV`. |
| lich        | Elder Lich       | **Phylactery** тАФ unlocks at boss lvl 3; free Heart item (200 HP, heart-full sprite), 4th life. 15% per-adv hunt roll on entry. Only one heart, no replacement if destroyed; with no normal lives, every party hunts the heart. **Necromancy** тАФ kills raise as free Skeletons next dawn (last 1 full day, retain class abilities, dead Clerics heal your minions, no minion-cap). | 1b.4 / 1b.5 | тЬЕ DONE (2026-05-02) тАФ Phylactery (1b.4) + Necromancy (1b.5) both shipped this pass | **Phylactery (1b.4):** new `src/data/items.json` registered in Preload; `BuildMenu` `_itemDefs()` filters by archetype + `unlockLevel` + one-per-run, hidden once placed. Items tab now also re-renders on `BOSS_LEVELED_UP` / `PHYLACTERY_PLACED` / `PHYLACTERY_DESTROYED` so the heart appears/disappears live. `NightPhase._confirmItemPlacement` validates non-boss room + floor tile, stamps `gameState.phylactery = { instanceId, roomId, tileX, tileY, worldX, worldY, resources: { hp, maxHp }, spriteKey, placedDay }`. New `PhylacteryRenderer` paints `heart-full` sprite + 28px HP bar with hurt-flash; instantiated in `Game.js` and ticked each frame. `BossSystem._endFight` was extended: when `winner='party'` drains `deathsRemaining` to 0 AND `phylactery.resources.hp > 0`, the system bumps `deathsRemaining` back to 1 and refills boss HP, swallowing the final-death event and emitting `PHYLACTERY_REVIVED_BOSS` instead. AISystem: new `HUNT_PHYLACTERY` goal type wired into `_goalToTile` (path target = phyl tile; falls back to FLEE if heart gone) and `_onGoalReached` (freeze adv on arrival; only re-pick when heart destroyed). `BossArchetypeSystem._onAdvsSpawned` rolls `LICH_PHYLACTERY_HUNT_CHANCE` (0.15) per adv on dungeon entry тАФ or forces 100% when `boss.deathsRemaining тЙд 0`. New `tick(delta)` runs from `Game.update()` real-time: every `LICH_PHYLACTERY_DMG_INTERVAL_MS` (800 ms), advs adjacent to the heart's tile with `HUNT_PHYLACTERY` deal `stats.attack` damage; when HP hits 0 the system fires `PHYLACTERY_DESTROYED` once, drops `gameState.phylactery`, and routes surviving hunters to FLEE. Unlock toast (`PHYLACTERY_UNLOCKED`) fires on `BOSS_LEVELED_UP` (and on scene boot for save-load) the first time `boss.level тЙе 3`; gated by `boss._lich.unlockToastShown`. `BossArchetypeUI` consumes that event + `PHYLACTERY_REVIVED_BOSS` + `PHYLACTERY_DESTROYED` and shows toasts. New balance constants: `LICH_PHYLACTERY_UNLOCK_LEVEL`, `LICH_PHYLACTERY_HUNT_CHANCE`, `LICH_PHYLACTERY_DMG_INTERVAL_MS`. **Necromancy (1b.5):** `_onAdvDied` queues `{ classId, name, level, tileX, tileY }` onto `gameState._lich.pendingRaises` whenever the active boss is the lich. `_onDayBegan` (DAY_PHASE_BEGAN listener) culls expired raised first via `_cullExpiredRaised` (cull rule: `today < m._expireAtDay`), then drains the pending queue via `_raiseQueuedDead`: spawns `skeleton1` via `createMinion` at the boss-chamber center (offset around a small ring so they don't stack), with `class: 'garrison'` (so they don't count toward the roster cap), `isUndead: true` (so MinionAISystem.respawnAll permanently removes them on death), `_raisedFromAdvDeath: true`, `_raisedClassId`, `_raisedAdvName`, `_expireAtDay = today + NECROMANCY_LIFESPAN_DAYS` (1, so they vanish at the very next dawn). `_applyClassRetentionBuffs` adjusts base stats per the dead adv's class (cleric: +DEF, range 2, support tag; mage: +ATK, range 3, arcane damage; ranger: +ATK, range 3; knight: +HP +DEF; barbarian: +ATK -DEF; monk: +SPD; rogue: +ATK +SPD; others: +1 ATK). Boss-level scaling re-applied on top via `applyBossLevelToMinion`. Raised cleric heal: `_tickRaisedClerics` runs each frame from `tick(delta)`, every `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_INTERVAL_MS` (2200) heals the most-wounded ally minion within Manhattan dist 3 for `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_AMOUNT` (4). Events: `NECROMANCY_RAISED { count, minionIds }`, `NECROMANCY_RAISED_EXPIRED { count }`, `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL { sourceId, targetId, amount }`. New balance constants: `NECROMANCY_LIFESPAN_DAYS`, `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_AMOUNT`, `NECROMANCY_CLERIC_HEAL_INTERVAL_MS`. |
| lizardman   | Serpent Captain  | **Camouflage** тАФ minions/traps invisible to advs until first attack (per-entity individual reveal); player sees them slightly transparent. **Venom Stack** тАФ every minion attack adds a -1 HP/sec poison stack; persists until adv dies or leaves dungeon; green tint + stack count VFX | 1b.6 | тЬЕ DONE (2026-05-02) | **Camouflage:** added `lizardman` tag to lizardman1/lizardman2 in minionTypes.json. `BossArchetypeSystem._onMinionPlaced` stamps `_camouflaged = true` on freshly placed lizardman-tagged minions while archetype is lizardman. `CombatSystem.tryAttack` clears the flag on the attacker's first hit and emits `LIZARDMAN_CAMO_REVEAL`. AISystem's `_findEngageableMinion` skips camouflaged minions (advs literally can't see them); `KnowledgeSystem.observeMinion` skips them too (no rumour-pool entry). MinionRenderer now multiplies container alpha by 0.5 when `_camouflaged` so the player sees a translucent ambusher. NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED listener re-camouflages every surviving lizardman minion so each new day = fresh ambush hit. Traps already invisible to advs by default (KnowledgeSystem only adds entries on `TRAP_TRIGGERED`), so no extra trap-side gate was needed. **Venom Stack:** new `_onCombatHit` listener тАФ when the source is a lizardman-tagged minion + the target is an active adv + damage > 0, increments `adv._venomStacks`. New `_tickVenom` runs from `tick(delta)` (always-on while archetype is lizardman); every `LIZARDMAN_VENOM_TICK_INTERVAL_MS` (1000) deals `stacks ├Ч LIZARDMAN_VENOM_DMG_PER_STACK` (1) to each poisoned adv via a synthetic `COMBAT_HIT` (sourceId='venom', damageType='poison'); fires `ADVENTURER_DIED` (killerId='venom') when the tick drops them. Stacks cleared on `ADVENTURER_FLED`. AdventurerRenderer paints a `Nx` green badge above the HP bar and tints the LPC sprite green while stacks > 0; clears tint + badge on stack drop. New balance constants: `LIZARDMAN_VENOM_TICK_INTERVAL_MS`, `LIZARDMAN_VENOM_DMG_PER_STACK`. |
| myconid     | Predator Myconid | **Spore Network** тАФ every 3 days all Corridor rooms emit a green spore cloud all day; 0.5├ЧbossLevel HP/tick to advs inside. **Corpse Bloom** тАФ adv corpses become green-tinted fungal terrain hazards for 3 days (-2 HP/sec on touch, stacks across corpses); after 3 days the corpse turns into a free Vinekin (`plant1`), no minion-cap. Despawn on room-move | 1b.7 | тЬЕ DONE (2026-05-02) | **Spore Network:** `_rollSporeNetwork` runs each `DAY_PHASE_BEGAN`; on days where `dayNumber % MYCONID_SPORE_INTERVAL_DAYS === 0` it stamps every corridor-room id (`starter_corridor` or any room tagged `corridor`) onto `gameState._myconid.activeSporeRoomIds`. `_renderSporeOverlay` paints a faint green wash + dotted edge + deterministic spore-speck dots on each room (depth 2.5 so the boss/minions still draw on top). `_tickMyconid` runs every frame from `tick(delta)`: every `MYCONID_SPORE_TICK_INTERVAL_MS` (1000), advs inside spore rooms take `Math.round(bossLevel ├Ч MYCONID_SPORE_DMG_PER_BOSS_LV)` damage, routed through COMBAT_HIT (sourceId='spores', damageType='poison'), with ADVENTURER_DIED on kill (killerId='spores'). New `FungalCorpseRenderer` paints each corpse: green wash + mossy ring + green-tinted skull glyph at the corpse tile, ticked from Game.update in both phases. `_tickMyconid` per frame: any adv standing on a corpse tile that hasn't already been listed in `adv._fungalCorpsesStung` adds the corpse id and bumps `adv._venomStacks` by `MYCONID_CORPSE_VENOM_STACKS_ADDED` (2) тАФ reusing the lizardman venom-tick pipeline (`_tickVenom` ungated so any archetype's stacks are processed). `_tickFungalCorpseDay` runs at every `DAY_PHASE_BEGAN`: decrements `daysRemaining` on each corpse and, when it hits zero, sprouts a free `plant1` (Vinekin) at the corpse tile via `createMinion` with `class: 'garrison'` (no minion-cap) + `_myconidSprout: true`, then removes the corpse from the list. `_onRoomRemovedMyconid` (subscribed to `ROOM_REMOVED`) drops every fungal corpse whose `roomId` matches the removed room. New balance constants: `MYCONID_SPORE_INTERVAL_DAYS`, `MYCONID_SPORE_DMG_PER_BOSS_LV`, `MYCONID_SPORE_TICK_INTERVAL_MS`, `MYCONID_CORPSE_LIFESPAN_DAYS`, `MYCONID_CORPSE_VENOM_STACKS_ADDED`. Corpse glyph **(updated 2026-05-02 polish pass):** `_onAdvDied` now captures the dead adv's `spriteVariant` (e.g. `knight/v01`) and the last-frame index of the `<key>-hurt-down` Phaser anim by walking `scene.anims.get(animKey).frames`. `FungalCorpseRenderer._createSprite` paints that exact frame from the LPC sheet at `0.55` scale, tinted `0x66ee66` тАФ so the corpse looks like the actual collapsed adv, just gone fungal. Falls back to the original green-tinted тШа glyph if the texture or frame isn't available (e.g. an adv without an LPC sprite). The wash + mossy ring underlay still renders in either case. |
| wraith      | Dark Wraith      | **Fear Meter** тАФ adv tracks fear (+5 corpse, +10 trap, +5 minion sighted, +15 ally died); 50%тЖТflee any random room, 75%тЖТattack other advs 5s, 100%тЖТdie (gold but no boss XP); floating bar VFX above adv (no overlap with HP bar). **Haunting** тАФ adv deaths spawn a free Ghost (`ghost2`) in that room (permanent, no minion-cap); patrols spawn room, sees advs in adjacent connected rooms, moves through walls to engage, returns home if alive | 1b.8 | тЬЕ DONE (2026-05-02) | **Fear Meter:** adv carries `_fear` (0..`WRAITH_FEAR_MAX`=100). `BossArchetypeSystem._addFear` clamps + emits `WRAITH_FEAR_CHANGED`. When in melee (dist тЙд 1) it calls `combatSystem.tryAttack(m, target)`. With no target it lerps back to its home tile (`_hauntPhase: 'home' / 'hunt' / 'return'`). Emits `WRAITH_HAUNT_SPAWNED` for any future UI hookups. `MINION_OBSERVED` event added to KnowledgeSystem тАФ fired only on first sighting per (adv, minion-type, room) tuple. Adv still loses HP as normal; lethal hits still kill them. Boss attacks unaffected. **VFX:** `BossArchetypeUI` listens for `VAMPIRE_CHARM_MARKED` (paints a pulsing dark-red ring around the charmed adv until conversion), `VAMPIRE_THRALL_CONVERTED` (cleans up the ring + toasts "A thrall joins your dungeon"), `VAMPIRE_BLOOD_TAX_TICK` (draws a red core + pink halo line from the adv to the boss for 450 ms). For each alive minion flagged as a patroller (`_isVampireThrall || _isDemonImp || _isHauntGhost`), it checks `dungeonGrid.getCpForDoorTile(tileX, tileY)`. On entering a fresh door tile it stores the cp on `m._doorPatLastCp` and snapshots `m._doorPatLockedSnapshot = !!cp.locked`, then calls `DungeonRenderer.openDoor(cp)` so the door visibly swings open during traversal. On stepping off the door tile it calls `DungeonRenderer.closeDoor(cp)` (which now mirrors to the paired cp on its own тАФ matching `openDoor`'s behavior) and restores `cp.locked = true` if the snapshot recorded it. Behavior is generic тАФ automatically benefits Vampire Thralls, Demon Imps, and Wraith Haunt Ghosts. Tracking state self-cleans on death/no-tag. |

| bard | Bard | 5b | тЬЕ DONE (re-audit 2026-05-22) | тЬЕ `bard_inspire` (+15% ATK aura, 2-tile, set duration) + тЬЕ `bard_speed` (+20% SPD aura, 2-tile, set duration) + тЬЕ `Encore` passive (`ABILITY_TRIGGERED { abilityId: 'encore' }` on bard death heals party 25%, gated by Crusader's Curse) тАФ all in `ClassAbilitySystem.js`. |

## 5. Dungeon mechanics (target: 13 from design + tons more)

**Active pact pool (2026-05-02):** **64 pacts** (added pact_of_the_marionette + completed all UI polish from prior batches: LongGamePopup wired into HudScene, SunderedFloorRenderer for telegraph/pit visuals, CartographerOverlay for adv-path dots, Jester name-scramble in BuildMenu trap tab, right-click-trap Brand selection + gold halo in TrapRenderer, 'C' hotkey + two-click Crucible sacrifice flow in NightPhase. Marionette possession: click-to-possess + WASD + auto-attack + camera follow + MinionAISystem suppression of other dungeon minions while possessed; releases on minion death / NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED / DAY_PHASE_STARTED.) **63 pacts** тАФ Phase 9 Batches AтАУH all shipped today. Original 13 (taxation_of_souls, bloodbound, gold_rush, undying_horde, sealed_paths, pack_synergy, blood_money, hasty_architect, great_erasure, schism, glory_hounds, sworn_rivals, famine_decree) + 50 new (Batch A: gilded_demise, pyramid_scheme, ransom_note, tax_the_living, tower_tax, crusaders_curse; Batch B: kennel_discipline, ironhide_rite, frenzy_pact, last_stand_doctrine, mage_hunt, vampires_toll; Batch C: tyrants_gaze, soul_tether, avengers_rite, final_breath; Batch D: false_maps, whispered_lies, open_book, whisperers_tongue; Batch E: doomsday_clock, the_long_game, inquisitors_mark; Batch F: summon_adds_i/ii/iii, drill_sergeant, endless_garrison, the_cull, trap_masons_touch, trapsmiths_guild, forbidden_workshop, architects_vision; Batch G: hellfire_breath, lightning_strike, shockwave_slam, spectral_reach, dark_vortex, soul_drain, doppelgangers, petrifying_stare; Batch H: cursed_soil, sundered_floor, pact_of_the_mirror, pact_of_the_cartographer, pact_of_the_jester, pact_of_the_whisperer, pact_of_the_brand, pact_of_the_reaper, pact_of_the_crucible). ### 5a. Damned Pacts тАФ solid-black tier (2026-05-28 тАФ тЬЕ all 24 implemented + headless-tested; 3 flow/UI ones flagged for playtest)

New **6th rarity tier** (`damned`, rendered solid black). Devil's-bargain pacts: `description` = the small one-time bribe (the green "Deal", paid in `onActivate`), `tradeoffDescription` = the huge permanent curse (the red "Price"). Schema is NOT inverted тАФ that mapping renders correctly in the existing Deal/Price UI. **Delivery:** 10% chance the Dark Pact grimoire is black тЖТ offers an all-Damned hand; otherwise Damned pacts mix into the normal pool at Epic draw weight (the tier just before Legendary тАФ weight 10). Permanent + unlimited stacking like normal pacts. Schema reuse тАФ no new fields. Gold-lump bribes are flat (values provisional, see DESIGN.md). Full spec lives in DESIGN.md ┬з "Damned Pacts". Tier wiring touches `PactCard.js` / `PactPicker.js` (add `damned` to RARITY maps + RARITY_GLYPH), `DungeonMechanicSystem._weightedSample` / `TIER_WEIGHTS` + `getOfferings`, and the DarkPact popup (`DarkPactPopup.js` / `PactPicker.js`) for the black-grimoire roll.

## 6. Dungeon room types

**Note (2026-04-30):** The original 9-room design list and the Phase-2/QW additions were **superseded by the Room redesign 2026-04-30** in DESIGN.md. The new spec defines 21 rooms organized around gateway/cap/scaling rules. Existing handler code for removed rooms remains in place as orphaned no-ops; cleanup is a follow-up phase.

### 6a. Required / Fixed

| ID | Name | Cap | Unlock | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| boss_chamber | Boss Chamber | 1 (fixed) | Start | 2 | тЬЕ DONE | fixed centerpiece, kept |
| entry_hall | Entry Hall | 1 / 2 / 3 (forced) | Start; L5; L10 | 3 | тЬЕ DONE | required entrance; multi-entry (2026-05-20) тАФ random per-adventurer spawn entry + flee-to-nearest, 2nd Entry Hall forced @ boss L5, 3rd @ L10 |

| ID | Name | Cap | Unlock | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| starter_corridor | Corridor | scales 2тЖТ20 (+2/level) | L1, free | 2 | тП│ PENDING (audit 2026-05-22) | Room exists, no behaviour. Cap-scaling-by-level still not implemented. |
| starter_barracks | Barracks | scales 1тЖТ5 | L1, free | 2 | ЁЯЯб PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | тЬЕ +10 roster slots per Barracks wired (`NightPhase.js` ~line 1714); тЬЕ sneakable behaviour data present; тЬЕ roster-vs-garrison minion split shipped (`Minion.js` `class` field defaults to `'roster'`, NightPhase enforces cap, garrison minions exempt). **Remaining**: per-Barracks 1тЖТ5 cap-scaling-by-level. |
| starter_guard_post | Guard Post | unlimited | L1 | TBD | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `MinionAISystem._pickTarget` adds a Guard-Post forward-operating-base check (`isGuardPost`) тАФ minions whose home room is a starter_guard_post engage adventurers in any room directly door-connected to the post, bypassing the same-room requirement but NOT escalating to whole-dungeon hunt. Existing `_walkAlongPath` handles cross-door travel; existing no-target return-home flow brings them back when the connected rooms clear. Garrison minions still hard-bound. |

| mimic_vault | Mimic Vault | 1 | L7 | TBD | тЬЕ DONE тАФ REWORKED 2026-05-22 | Disguised as Treasury; 2 chest-disguised mimics per day (state: 'chest'). Each mimic rolls a `chestTier` (1..10) at spawn тАФ MinionRenderer paints them as the matching `item-treasure-chest-<tier>` sprite with a red tint (`0xff5050`) for player visibility; adv AI ignores the tint. KnowledgeSystem.observeRoomContents adds disguised mimics to `adv.knowledge.treasureChests` with an `_isMimic` flag so the standard chest-tempt loop picks them up. `AISystem._tryTriggerMimic` (runs alongside `_tryOpenTreasureChest` on every tile step) springs an unknowing adv within 1 tile: `mimicStateтЖТ'sprung'`, MIMIC_SPRUNG emitted, all alive advs + sharedPool gain `knowledge.mimics[id]`, opener killed via `_kill`. `_resetSprungMimics` flips state back to 'chest' on NIGHT_PHASE_STARTED. Knowledge-aware advs see through the disguise (allow-list in MinionAISystem `_pickTarget` adv-side filter); MinionAISystem retaliation carve-out lets mimics swing back when attacked. The placeable Mimic minion (Barracks roster) uses the exact same path. *(Reworked from the original 40%/5% open-roll + 30% max-HP bite + reveal-and-engage mechanic тАФ replaced with stationary instant-kill trap per user 2026-05-22.)* |

| throne_room | Throne Room | scales 1тЖТ2 | L9 | TBD | тЬЕ DONE тАФ DEVIATION (audit 2026-05-22) | 1 Mini-Boss per Throne Room nightly, garrison/room-bound, stats scaled by current boss level via `MINION_HP_PER_BOSS_LV` + `MINION_ATK_PER_BOSS_LV` (`RoomBehaviorSystem.js` ~line 246). DEVIATION: original "T1тЖТT2тЖТT3 family progression" simplified to a fixed skeleton3 baseline whose stats scale instead. Visual family-swap is deferred polish; mechanic intent (escalating threat) is preserved via stat scaling. Noted in DESIGN.md 2026-05-22. |
| sanctum | Sanctum | 1 | L10 (capstone) | TBD | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Boss HP regen between fights: +8 HP per Sanctum per round (`BossSystem.js` ~line 1835). Minion regen aura: minions in any room door-connected to an active Sanctum get the barracks-style regen treatment (`MinionAISystem._isAdjacentToSanctum`). |

### 6d. Top-level rules (Room redesign 2026-04-30)

| Rule | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| Roster vs Garrison minion split | TBD | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `Minion.js` carries `class: 'roster' \| 'garrison'` (default `'roster'`). `NightPhase._rosterUsed/_rosterCap` enforces +10-per-Barracks cap; garrison minions (Crypt, Mimic Vault, Hall of Trials, Throne Room, Catacombs revenants) are excluded from the cap and AI-pinned to their `assignedRoomId`. |
| "Adjacent / connected" = direct shared door | TBD | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `dungeonGrid.getNeighborRooms(instanceId)` returns rooms that share a connection-point, not transitive тАФ consumed by Veil, Sanctum, Watchtower, Wandering Gate. |
| Alive-exit-required for chest/loot theft | TBD | ЁЯЪл SCOPE_CHANGED (audit 2026-05-22) | Original 4-chest Treasury + loot-pickup-on-escape model was retired 2026-05-02 in the loot-pickup cleanup. Treasury became a flat daily stipend; Mimic Vault became a chest-disguise-and-bite mechanic. The "alive-exit-required" rule is no longer relevant to the current design. |
| Cap scaling by boss level | TBD | ЁЯЯб PARTIAL (audit 2026-05-22) | Some scaling exists (throne-room mini-boss stats, library forecast size, beacon buff bonus). The unified per-room cap-scaling-by-level table from DESIGN.md is **not** implemented тАФ caps are mostly fixed-per-instance with +X-per-Room aggregation. |
| Boss level cap = 10 | TBD | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Boss level capped at 10 in current BossSystem. |

## 7. Trap types

**2026-05-20 redesign.** The original 3 standard + 9 interaction traps were scrapped тАФ none ever shipped (`trapTypes.json` was always `[]`; the old `TrapSystem`/`Trap`/`TrapRenderer` code targeted that dead roster). Replaced by the 8-trap roster below. Old rows preserved in git history.

### 7a. Current roster (8 traps) тАФ тЬЕ DONE

| ID | Name | Footprint | Placement | Trigger | Unlock | Gold | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| spike_pillar | Spike Pillar | 2├Ч2 | floor | adv within 1 tile | L3 | 20 | тЬЕ DONE |
| shooting_arrows | Shooting Arrows | 1 wall tile | wall (not doorway) | adv in LOS lane | L4 | 30 | тЬЕ DONE |
| rotating_blades | Rotating Blades | 2├Ч2 | floor | adv in adjacent tile | L4 | 25 | тЬЕ DONE |
| bomb | Bomb | 1├Ч1 | floor | adv within 2 tiles тЖТ 3s fuse | L5 | 35 | тЬЕ DONE |
| saw_blade | Saw Blade | 3-tile track | floor | saw overlaps adv | L6 | 35 | тЬЕ DONE |
| spike_pit | Spike Pit | 2├Ч2 | floor (fully interior) | stepped on | L6 | 40 | тЬЕ DONE |
| cannon | Cannon | 1├Ч1 | floor | adv in LOS (faced dir) | L7 | 45 | тЬЕ DONE |
| dragon_trap | Dragon Trap | 1 wall tile | wall (not doorway) | adv in LOS lane | L8 | 55 | тЬЕ DONE |

Locked specs: 1 Trap-Factory slot each; never in boss room / entry hall. Trap Factory (gateway room) unlocks at boss L3; traps unlock L3тАУ8. Trap damage scales +12%/boss level (`Balance.TRAP_DAMAGE_PER_BOSS_LV`); trap gold cost scales +20%/boss level (`Balance.TRAP_COST_PER_BOSS_LV`) тАФ both mirror the minion system. Gold values in `trapTypes.json` are the level-1 base. Knowledge gained only on trigger or damage-survived. Area/contact hazards hit both factions; LOS projectile traps hit adventurers only and are confined to the trap's own room (lane stops at walls/doors).

### 7b. Cross-cutting infrastructure (new тАФ none of this existed) тАФ тЬЕ DONE

| Item | Phase | Status |
|---|---|---|
| Multi-tile (2├Ч2) footprint + placement validation | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Wall-mounted placement category + auto-door suppression | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Trap collision (solid-tile registration for pathfinding) | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Line-of-sight scan (room-confined; canned projectile animations) | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Proximity / radius / adjacent-contact triggers | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Continuous-damage zones (blades / saw / pillar) | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Moving trap (saw track travel тАФ time-based wave) | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Trap rotation + R-key handling (cannon only) | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Poison damage-over-time status effect | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Bomb fuse countdown + 5-tile-radius explosion + chain | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Knowledge gain (trigger / damage-survived) тЖТ pathfinder routing | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Trap damage scales with boss level (+12%/lvl) | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |
| Rewrite `Trap.js` / `TrapSystem.js` / `TrapRenderer.js` (old roster) | TRAPS | тЬЕ DONE |

## 27. Dungeon-content placements (other than rooms/minions/traps)

| Item | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|
| Mini-bosses (placeable, guard rooms) | 7b | тЬЕ DONE тАФ minion placed in treasure_room auto-promotes (3├Ч HP, 1.6├Ч attack), guarantees high-tier drop on death |
| Hidden keys | QW | тЬЕ DONE | RoomBehaviorSystem._onNightStart drops an iron_key in a random non-boss room each night when a locked room exists but no key is on the floor |
| Locked doors | QW | тЬЕ DONE | KnowledgeSystem.costMultiplierForTile returns 9999 for tiles inside locked rooms when adventurer lacks an iron_key тАФ A* effectively treats them as impassable |
| Secret rooms | QW | тЬЕ DONE | secret_passage room type; AISystem._pickNextGoal filters out secret rooms unless adv has `mapper` or `completionist` tag |
| Adventurer level scales with boss level | 7b | тЬЕ DONE тАФ +10% maxHp, +7% attack per boss level above 1 (applied in DayPhase spawn via ADVENTURER_HP_PER_BOSS_LV / ADVENTURER_ATK_PER_BOSS_LV) |
| Boss level progression (rooms unlock, minions scale) | 7b | тЬЕ DONE тАФ Boss owns level/xp/xpToNext (moved from meta). Each kill awards BOSS_XP_PER_KILL (10) XP; levels up at curve 100├Ч1.5^(lv-1). Cap 10. BOSS_LEVELED_UP event expands grid + retroactively scales all live minions (+10% HP / +7% ATK per level). Replaces dungeon-level system (2026-05-01). |
| Minions scale with boss level | тАФ | тЬЕ DONE тАФ applyBossLevelToMinion() applied at spawn, on evolution reset, and retroactively on BOSS_LEVELED_UP. Same +10% HP / +7% ATK curve as adventurers. |
| "Legendary heroes" tier (drawn by high reputation) | 10 | тЬЕ DONE | DayPhase rolls ReputationSystem.legendarySpawnChance() per spawn; isLegendary flag + 1.5├ЧHP / 1.4├ЧATK / 1.3├ЧDEF |
| Guild raid teams (full party of coordinated adventurers) | 10b | тЬЕ DONE | DayPhase._spawnDailyAdventurers branches to a 4-person raid path at feared+ reputation (or whenever runConfig.allRaids is set); shared partyId, +25% HP/atk, 2 personalities each |

## 30. Sprite-based dungeon tiling тАФ themes + tileset editor + room template editor

> See DESIGN.md тЖТ "Sprite-based dungeon tiling" for the full spec.
> Three-phase build (A тЖТ B тЖТ C). Each row "data + UI + persistence + game wiring".

| ID | Item | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| theme-schema | Theme JSON schema (slots: floor, 10 wall slots, 24 door slots; per-slot variant arrays) | 30A | тЬЕ DONE тАФ DEVIATION (audit 2026-05-22) | `assets/themes/manifest.json` lists 40+ tile sprites (walls, pillars, doors, corners, floors 1-31, dirt floors, wall holes) loaded via `Preload`. Per-room theme indirection skipped тАФ see `theme-per-room` row. |
| sprite-library | Sprite library (PNGs + per-sprite metadata: srcSize 32/64/128, mode scale\|span, tags) | 30A | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `assets/themes/sprites/*.png` + `assets/themes/manifest.json`; loaded as `themesprite-<id>` texture keys in `Preload.js`. |
| variant-pick | Random pick per cell at dungeon-build time, persisted in dungeon state (no per-frame flicker) | 30A | ЁЯЪл SCOPE_CHANGED (audit 2026-05-22) | Replaced by explicit per-cell authoring: every room's `tileLayout` in `rooms.json` names the exact sprite per cell. No runtime random variant pick needed. |
| fs-handle | File System Access API wrapper (pick project root once, persist handle in IndexedDB, write PNGs + JSON) | 30A | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Used by both `TilesetEditor.js` and `RoomTileEditor.js` to write changes back to disk. |
| tileset-editor | TilesetEditor scene: sprite library panel, slot grid w/ variants, scale/span toggle, live preview, save theme | 30A | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `src/scenes/TilesetEditor.js`. Reached from the MainMenu TILESET EDITOR rune (cheat-name-gated). |
| theme-per-room | Each room template in rooms.json gets a `theme: "<name>"` field | 30A | ЁЯЪл SCOPE_CHANGED (audit 2026-05-22) | Per-room `theme:` indirection abandoned in favour of direct per-cell `tileLayout` authoring on each room. 0/21 rooms currently carry a `theme` field. |
| room-tile-editor | RoomTileEditor scene: load any room template, paint cells with library sprites, save tileLayout back to rooms.json | 30B | тЬЕ DONE | uses existing `tileLayout` field on rooms.json |
| room-tile-rotation | Per-cell rotation in RoomTileEditor: R-key / UI button cycles brush 0/90/180/270; cell entries become `string \| { id, rot }`; renderer applies setAngle | 30B+ | тЬЕ DONE | scope (1) only тАФ per-variant rotation in TilesetEditor not yet planned |
| room-tile-mirror | Per-cell horizontal + vertical mirror toggles on the brush. Cell entries gain optional `flipH`, `flipV` booleans; renderer applies image.flipX / flipY. Composes with rotation. | 30B+ | тП│ PENDING | brush state persists across MainMenu round-trips like rotation does |
| renderer-sprite-path | DungeonRenderer adds sprite-based tile path; consumes active theme + per-cell overrides; falls back to procedural when no theme | 30C | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | `DungeonRenderer` paints rooms from their `tileLayout` (string \| `{id, rot}` per cell) using `themesprite-<id>` textures and the `_themeTextureKey()` helper. Falls back to procedural when no layout. |
| span-rendering | Renderer honors span sprites: 64 covers 2├Ч2 anchor, 128 covers 4├Ч4; covered cells skipped | 30C | тП│ PENDING | Not yet implemented тАФ current per-cell pipeline assumes 32px tiles only. Low priority unless larger sprites land. |
| mainmenu-runes | MainMenu gets TILESET EDITOR + ROOM EDITOR runes | 30A/B | тЬЕ DONE (audit 2026-05-22) | Both runes present in `MainMenuOverlay`, gated behind the `'mango'` cheat name. |

## 32. Adventurer emote bubbles (2026-05-01)

| ID | Item | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| emote-assets | Copy 60 emote PNGs from staging into `assets/sprites/emotes/`; each is 96├Ч32 with three 32├Ч32 frames | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | filenames map to triggers |
| emote-preload | Register emote spritesheets in Preload.js; build a manifest mapping triggerId тЖТ variant texture keys | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | catalog lives in EmoteSystem.js, Preload imports `allEmoteVariants` |
| emote-system | `EmoteSystem.js` тАФ subscribes to trigger events, rolls 20% chance, attaches sprite to adv container at yтЙИ-52, plays once, destroys | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | per-adv cooldown 1500ms; priority replaces lower/equal |
| emote-trigger-random | Ambient `random_exploring` roll while walking (~6тАУ10s window, 20% chance) | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | low priority тАФ never overrides state emote |
| emote-trigger-rooms | Hook `ROOM_OBSERVED` тАФ `firstVisit:true` тЖТ discovered/unknown pool; `firstVisit:false` тЖТ known-room pool | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | KnowledgeSystem already emits both flavors |
| emote-trigger-combat | Hook fighting state transition тЖТ `fighting + found minion + class-specific` pool, filtered by classId | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | tracked via aiState change in update tick |
| emote-trigger-flee | Hook fleeing state / `ADVENTURER_FLED` тЖТ fleeing pool | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | aiState/`goal.type === FLEE` edge-trigger |
| emote-trigger-low-hp | Hook HP fraction crossing below 30% тЖТ low_health pool | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | edge-trigger only |
| emote-trigger-loot | Hook `MIMIC_REVEAL_TRIGGERED` and `TREASURY_CHEST_GRAB_STARTED` тЖТ found_loot pool | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | gear pickup deprecated |
| emote-trigger-trap | Hook `TRAP_TRIGGERED` тЖТ found_something pool | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | |
| emote-trigger-boss | Hook `BOSS_FIGHT_INCOMING` тЖТ entered_boss_room | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | |
| emote-trigger-tame | Hook `MINION_TAMED` тЖТ tame_success | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | |
| emote-trigger-resurrect | Hook `ADVENTURER_RESURRECTED` тЖТ resurrected | 32 | тЬЕ DONE | |

## 33. Dungeon events (2026-05-05)

> See DESIGN.md тЖТ "Dungeon events" for full per-event spec. All events are pre-announced during the night phase before the day they fire (Dark Deal + Loot Goblin Heist resolve during the night phase itself).

| ID | Item | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| event-system | `EventSystem` тАФ schedule + roll engine, event registry, night-phase notification banner, JSON-driven event definitions in `src/data/events.json` | EV | тЬЕ DONE | **Cadence (revised 2026-05-21): first event day 3, then every 3 days (was 6тАУ8). Same event cannot fire back-to-back. Speed Runner / Rival Dungeon gated to boss level тЙе 3; every event also carries a per-event `minBossLevel`.** (The Tournament was removed 2026-05-21 тАФ see `event-tournament`.) |
| event-guild-raid | Guild Raid! тАФ next day spawns 2├Ч adventurers as steady pressure (longer wave, not one-shot surge) | EV | тЬЕ DONE | |
| event-legendary-speedrunner | Legendary Speed Runner тАФ single 2├Ч stats / 2├Ч speed adventurer, ignores non-essential rooms + minions, beelines to boss; killing them grants massive boss XP | EV | тЬЕ DONE | Boss level тЙе 3. Name intentionally fourth-wall-breaking. Pathfind: shortest path to boss room, only engages chokepoint-required minions. |
| event-pestilence | Dungeon Pestilence тАФ minions start day at 50% HP; melee with adventurer applies "Blighted" DoT until they die or leave; affects existing + newly-placed minions; Blight does NOT persist after adv leaves | EV | тЬЕ DONE | Adds new status: `blighted` on adventurer entity. |

## 34. UI / HUD overhaul v2 тАФ claude-design DOM port (2026-05-18)

> Second pass on the HUD chrome. Section 31's Phaser-rendered Crypt-themed implementation ships and stays default until each panel here lands. Source design files: `D:\Documents\Game Jam Code\Quest-Failed assets\claude design ui\design_handoff_quest_failed_ui\` (high-fidelity HTML/React/CSS mockups; the README in that folder is the source of truth for tokens, animations, and panel layout). Render strategy: DOM overlay on top of the Phaser canvas, vanilla JS modules in `src/hud/`, no build step. A 1920├Ч1080 logical stage is transform-scaled to fit the viewport so design coordinates stay literal. Gated behind a feature flag (`?newhud=1` URL param or `localStorage.newhud='1'`) until every Phase 34B panel has shipped тАФ then the flag flips default-on and section 31 chrome moves to removed-not-deleted.

| ID | Item | Phase | Status | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|

Singleton `window.__game._hudRoot` so scene-restarts don't re-mount. |

## 35. Companion NPC тАФ Lilith (2026-05-21)

> Persistent in-HUD succubus companion who reacts to everything the player does and everything that happens in the dungeon, delivers the tutorials, and breaks the fourth wall. Bottom-left peeking portrait + RPG chat bubble. Personality: flirty + wicked with a sarcastic/sinister edge. 42 hand-drawn expression sprites. Data-driven line bank. Hideable via a 3-way Off/Quiet/Normal option. Source sprites: `D:\Documents\Game Jam Code\Quest-Failed assets\Main NPC` (42 PNGs).

## 39. Fourth companion тАФ Safira (2026-05-22)

> The fourth and final companion, **Safira** тАФ a chaotic, dazzling wish-granting genie. Personality: manic over-eagerness, frames the player's actions as "wishes" she grants, swings between giddy delight and theatrical panic; breaks the fourth wall harder than any other companion (direct & intimate, vs Zul'Gath's serene detachment). Addresses the player as "Master". Built the same way as the others; full parallel dialogue bank. Sits 3rd of 4 on the recruit screen (between Malakor and Zul'Gath), facing right. Source sprites: `Quest-Failed assets/Main NPC 4 - Safira` (53 PNGs). Completes the companion roster.

## 40. Unlockable companions + Nocturna lock-screen (2026-05-25)

> Roster expands beyond the original four. The original four ship unlocked; future companions are gated behind player progression (unlock conditions TBD per companion). The CompanionSelect screen keeps the original full-size cards and **paginates** the roster тАФ three companions visible at a time, flanked by тЧА / тЦ╢ arrows. Locked companions still render at full size тАФ silhouette-tinted portrait with a padlock badge тАФ so the player sees the character teased but not their dialogue / personality. First locked companion: **Nocturna** (moonlit cat-girl witch, idle portrait only тАФ full implementation deferred). Source art: `Quest-Failed assets/Main NPC 5 - Nocturna`.

| cmp-spectra-unlock-condition | **Wired 2026-05-27.** Spectra is unlocked by the new `flawless_reign` legendary achievement: survive 30 days in a single run without the boss taking any damage. Title reward: **The Flawless**. AchievementSystem fires `PlayerProfile.unlockCompanion('spectra')` when the threshold is met (same plumbing as Zul'Gath / Rattle Bones). STRICT damage definition тАФ any HP loss from any source invalidates the run's no-hit streak | 40 | тЬЕ DONE | `BossSystem._applyDamageToBoss` now emits a `BOSS_DAMAGED` event; AchievementSystem subscribes to that plus `SUMMON_ADD_DEATH_BOSS_TOLL` and `PACT_BOSS_LIGHTNING_FIRED.selfCost`. New per-run flag `bossEverDamagedThisRun` flips on the first hit and freezes the no-hit day-counter for the rest of the run. |

---

## 41. Achievements (2026-05-25)

> 45-achievement progression layer surfacing milestones + gating content unlocks. Reachable from the main menu + from per-row chips on the leaderboard (Phase C). Boss-level achievements (lvl 1тАУ20) cover most of the slots; 25 non-level achievements span onboarding тЖТ mastery. Hoard Lord (10k gold in one run) unlocks Zul'Gath, who's now locked at first-boot.

| ach-visual-polish | Visual polish pass after user feedback that the overlay was "way too much yellow." The mango cheat's "everything unlocked" state now reads as a rich tapestry instead of a gold sea тАФ the original user complaint that drove this pass. | ach-compare-toggle-inline | "COMPARE WITH YOU" toggle (viewer-mode only) moved from `position: absolute; top: 30px; right: 24px` (a relic from the full-screen layout that put it on top of the LEADERBOARD button in the smaller popup) to inline-flow in the header flex row beside the counter | 41 | тЬЕ DONE | One CSS change тАФ drop `position / top / right`. | ach-legendary-toast | Legendary unlocks (the 6 hand-picked achievements with `def.legendary === true`) get a tier-aware toast that's visually distinct from common unlocks: RARE TROPHY eyebrow above the title, "LEGENDARY UNLOCKED" header (instead of "ACHIEVEMENT UNLOCKED"), gold-bright frame with 2px border + ember inset glow + 2.2s pulse animation, larger glyph (22px) + larger title (13px), 10s dwell (vs 5s for common toasts). Plus a 22-particle gold burst spawned alongside тАФ each particle absolute-positioned within the toast, animated via CSS keyframes with per-particle inline `--dx` / `--dy` trajectory vars, biased to a 120┬░ leftward arc so particles fountain INTO the play area instead of off the right screen edge. Auto-cleanup after 1.3s | 41 | тЬЕ DONE | New `legendary_achievement` kind in ToastQueue's KIND_STYLE; `_spawnLegendaryBurst(toastEl)` method spawns the particle ring. Legendary tier is now data-driven via `def.legendary` in `achievements.json` (was previously a hardcoded `LEGENDARY_IDS` Set in AchievementsOverlay.js тАФ the JS reads `def.legendary` too now so the grid card's shimmer treatment and the toast's tier branching share the same source of truth). |
| ach-title-picker-cleanup | Audit found a HIGH-severity bug: title-picker outside-click handler was leaking when the player closed the achievements overlay while the picker was open. The handler stayed bound to the document and could fire against stale element refs on the next overlay session. Fix: centralized teardown in `_onOverlayClose` (now used as the Overlay shell's onClose callback) which removes the keydown listener + outside-click handler + tears down the nested viewer overlay all in one path | 41 | тЬЕ DONE | Surfaced by an Explore-agent audit pass. Same teardown now fires whether the overlay closes via close-X, Esc, or backdrop click. |

## How to keep this file honest

- **At every phase exit**: update statuses for items tagged in that phase. If a row is still PENDING or PARTIAL when the phase ends, either fix it or get explicit user approval to defer.
- **When the user adds new design items**: add them here with phase + status before implementing.
- **Open-ended (ЁЯТн) items**: track running counts in the relevant section (e.g. "12/30 mechanics shipped").
- **When implementation differs from design**: don't silently rewrite this file тАФ flag the divergence to the user and update DESIGN.md if they approve.
